        function cdnfallback() {
            if (window.appInsights) {
                var region = "West Europe";
                var siteName = "acom-prod-westeurope-02";
                var error = new Error('Bundle - client side cdn fallback to local cdn, region: ' + region + ' , sitename: ' + siteName);

                window.appInsights.trackException({ exception: error });
            }

            if (window.location.search.indexOf('cdn=disable') === -1) {
                window.location.href = '?cdn=disable';
            }
        }

  <script>

    $(window).on('load', function () {
        function enableSSO() {
            setTimeout(function () {
                window.addEventListener("message", receiveMessage, false);
                var iframe = document.createElement('iframe');
                iframe.src = '/auth/sso/';
                iframe.setAttribute('id', 'sso-frame');
                iframe.setAttribute('style', 'width: 0; height: 0; border: 0; border: none; position: absolute;');
                iframe.setAttribute('aria-hidden', true);
                $('body').prepend(iframe);
            }, 500);
        }

        function receiveMessage(event) {
            if (event.origin !== 'https://azure.microsoft.com' || event.data !== 'sso-success') {
            return;
            }

            
            window.setTimeout(function () { document.getElementById('sso-frame').contentWindow.location.replace('/auth/sso/'); }, 30 * 60 * 1000);

            
            var enabledSubmitInputs = $('input:enabled[type="submit"], button:enabled[type="submit"]');
            enabledSubmitInputs.attr('disabled', true);

            window.dispatchEvent(createNewEvent('sso.success')); 

            
            $.ajax({ url: '/auth/sso/info/', timeout: 3000 })
                .done(function (data) {
                    if (data) {
                        $('.auth-container').html(data);
                    }
                })
                .fail(function () {
                    
                    enabledSubmitInputs.attr('disabled', false);
                });

            
            $.ajax({ url: '/auth/antiforgerytoken/', timeout: 3000 })
                .done(function (data) {
                    $('input[name="__RequestVerificationToken"]').replaceWith(data);
                    window.dispatchEvent(createNewEvent('sso.requestVerificationTokenReceived'));
                })
                .always(function () {
                    
                    enabledSubmitInputs.attr('disabled', false);
                });
        }

        
        function createNewEvent(eventName) {
            var event;

            if (typeof (Event) === 'function') {
                event = new Event(eventName);
            } else {
                event = document.createEvent('Event'); 
                event.initEvent(eventName, true, true);
            }

            return event;
        }

        // We won't process requests made from any status page
        if (window.location.pathname.indexOf('/status/') === -1)
        {
            // enable sso only if the userAgent is not safari
            if (!/^((?!chrome|android).)*safari/i.test(navigator.userAgent)) {
                enableSSO();
            }
        }
    });

</script>

     <div class="column large-4 large-pull-8 medium-5 medium-pull-7"> 
      <h2>Boost productivity with machine learning for all skill levels</h2> 
      <p>Szybko twórz i wdra?aj modele uczenia maszynowego za pomoc? narz?dzi spe?niaj?cych Twoje oczekiwania bez wzgl?du na poziom umiej?tno?ci. U?ywaj wbudowanych notesów Jupyter Notebook z funkcj? IntelliSense lub <a href="/pl-pl/services/machine-learning/designer/">projektanta</a> przeci?gania i upuszczania. Przyspieszaj tworzenie modeli za pomoc? <a href="/pl-pl/services/machine-learning/automatedml/">zautomatyzowanego uczenia maszynowego</a> i u?ywaj zaawansowanych opcji in?ynierii funkcji, wybierania algorytmów oraz czyszczenia hiperparametrów. Zwi?ksz efektywno?? zespo?u dzi?ki udost?pnionym zestawom danych, notesom, modelom i pulpitom nawigacyjnym z mo?liwo?ci? dostosowywania, które ?ledz? wszystkie aspekty procesu uczenia maszynowego.</p>

    <div class="row row-size8"> 
     <div class="column medium-7"> 
      <img src="//azurecomcdn.azureedge.net/cvt-526390d16d87de1877250c5808f92a928069f41676f250913969acdedd7e9a4a/images/page/services/machine-learning/value-prop-2.png" class="device-wrapper" alt=""> 
     </div> 
     <div class="column medium-5 large-4 large-offset-1"> 
      <h2>Operacjonalizacja na du?? skal? dzi?ki metodyce MLOps</h2> 
      <p>Take advantage of <a href="/pl-pl/services/machine-learning/mlops/">MLOps</a> to streamline the machine learning lifecycle, from building models to deployment and management. Create reproducible workflows with machine learning pipelines, and train, validate, and deploy thousands of models at scale, from the cloud to the edge. Use managed online and batch endpoints to seamlessly deploy and score models without managing the underlying infrastructure. Use Azure DevOps or GitHub Actions to schedule, manage, and automate the machine learning pipelines, and use advanced data-drift analysis to improve model performance over time.</p> 
     </div> 
    </div>
